Parking is free for guests staying in the hotel, but if you park for more than 48 hours, you need to drive the car out and drive it back. It is said that it is a system problem. We stayed in the hotel again during the Spring Festival in 2024, and no parking fee was charged. [Environment] The hotel was opened in 2017. We always choose the elegant building. The rooms in the elegant building are apartment-type. The rooms are spacious and clean. The rooms are equipped with a living room. Although it has been open for so many years, the stay experience is as good as always. Next to the hotel is Tongcheng Outlets, which is super convenient for shopping and dining. Well, you can eat at Fire Palace. There is also a Wanda Cinema on the 2nd floor next to the hotel. [Price] The price during the National Day is more than 400. For an Internet celebrity city like Changsha, this price is already super cost-effective. During the Spring Festival in 2024, breakfast is not included, and the cost is about 400 yuan, which is super cost-effective. Breakfast can be had at Fire Palace next to the hotel, as well as KFC and McDonald's. [Other configurations] The hotel has a swimming pool, but it is a bit troublesome to go to the swimming pool if you live in the elegant building. You have to take the elevator. The swimming pool is not heated, and it is still a bit cold to swim in October. The shallowest water depth of the pool is 1.3 meters. There is a fee to rent a swimming ring, but the fee is not high. I forgot whether it is 10 yuan or 20 yuan~ [Service] We arrived at the hotel at 8 o'clock in the evening, and the check-in was very fast. We stayed for 3 nights, and the cleaning was also very efficient~ During the Spring Festival, we also stayed for 3 nights, checking in on the fifth day of the first ***** month and leaving on the eighth day of the first ***** month
